class="LayoutContainer_container__O1X6V Article_body__W1ljI" data-component="LayoutContainer"><div><div><p class="paragraph_paragraph__3Hrfa">From under the sea to a bush toilet, the beauty of nature can be found everywhere as these talented photographers have revealed. </p><p class="paragraph_paragraph__3Hrfa">Winners from across Australia have been celebrated for their stunning shots in the 2023 Australian Geographic Nature Photographer of the Year. </p><p class="paragraph_paragraph__3Hrfa">Marking 20 years of the competition, Australian Geographic picture editor Nicky Catley said the images also depicted the &quot;fragility of our natural world&quot;.</p><p class="paragraph_paragraph__3Hrfa">&quot;The competition has become a record of our changing world, an earth in perpetual transformation, and this year we recognise that photography is more important than ever in showing us what is at risk of being lost,&quot; Ms Catley said.</p><p class="paragraph_paragraph__3Hrfa">There were 11 categories this year, including: </p><ul class="ContentAlignment_marginBottom__jDkGS ContentAlignment_overflowVisible__1Fb_1 List_unordered__TB6BG"
